folium.plugins.MeasureControl() 

from folium.plugins import MeasureControl
m = folium.Map([35.84694109945701, 127.12941011336521],
               zoom_start=17,
               scrollWheelZoom=False)
m.add_child(folium.plugins.MeasureControl())
m

folium.plugins.TimestampedGeoJson 

a1=[35.847336682624395, 127.13066143667929]
a2=[35.847163718642705, 127.12985784659246]
a3=[35.8466227437543, 127.13004852898592]
a4=[35.845842555784095, 127.13032547246222]
a5=[35.84567326870173, 127.13185547166708]
a1.reverse()
a2.reverse()
a3.reverse()
a4.reverse()
a5.reverse()
t1='2021-11-21 12:00:00'
t2='2021-11-21 12:05:00'
t3='2021-11-21 12:10:00'
t4='2021-11-21 12:15:00'
t5='2021-11-21 12:20:00'


points = [
    {
        "time": t1,
        "coordinates": a1,
    },
    {
        "time": t2,
        "coordinates": a2,
    },
    {
        "time": t3,
        "coordinates": a3,
    },
    {
        "time": t4,
        "coordinates": a4,
    },
    {
        "time": t5, 
        "coordinates": a5
    },
]

features = [
    {
        "type": "Feature",
        "geometry": {
            "type": "LineString",
            "coordinates": [
                a1,
                a2,
                a3,
                a4,
                a5,
            ],
        },
        "properties": {
            "times": [
                t1,
                t2,
                t3,
                t4,
                t5,
            ],
            "icon": "circle",
            "iconstyle": {
                "fillColor": "green",
                "fillOpacity": 0.6,
                "stroke": "false",
                "radius": 13,
            },
            "style": {"weight": 0},
            "id": "man",
        },
    }
]

m = folium.Map([35.84694109945701, 127.12941011336521],
               zoom_start=17,
               scrollWheelZoom=False)

folium.plugins.TimestampedGeoJson(
    {"type": "FeatureCollection", "features": features},
    period="PT1M",
    add_last_point=True,
).add_to(m)

m

                        }
          } for line in lines]

folium.plugins.TimestampedGeoJson({
    'type':'FeatureCollection',
    'features':features,
}, period='PT30S', add_last_point=True).add_to(m)
m

import numpy as np
data = (
    np.random.normal(size=(100, 3)) *
    np.array([[1, 1, 1]]) +
    np.array([[28, 77, 1]])
).tolist()
m = folium.Map(tiles='OpenStreetMap', zoom_start=15,scrollWheelZoom=False)
folium.plugins.HeatMap(data).add_to(m)
m

N = 100 #Number of Popups
#Generate Random Datasets
data = np.array(
    [
        np.random.uniform(low=11, high=33, size=N),  
        np.random.uniform(low=70, high=88, size=N),  
    ]
).T
popups = [str(i) for i in range(N)] # Popups texts are simple numbers.
#Create a Map
randomPopupMarker_Map = folium.Map([27, 77], zoom_start=4,scrollWheelZoom=False)
plugins.MarkerCluster(data, popups=popups).add_to(randomPopupMarker_Map)
randomPopupMarker_Map

import folium.plugins as plugins
title= '''<h3 align="center">전주여행</h3>'''
#Define the map
IndiaTourMap = folium.Map(location=[35.81, 127.145], zoom_start=14, tiles="cartodbpositron",scrollWheelZoom=False)
#Define the coordinates
coords = [
    [35.812654484847336, 127.14712754226657],
    [35.81325957796508, 127.1492877845946],
    [35.81601233748957, 127.15464802956764],
    [35.819915980165995, 127.14449439808683],
    [35.797428476068575, 127.1228218269223]
]
#Let us add color code connects for each coordinates
plugins.PolyLineOffset(
    coords, weight=2, dash_array="5,10", color="red", opacity=1
).add_to(IndiaTourMap)
plugins.PolyLineOffset(coords, color="#00f", opacity=0.5, offset=-5).add_to(IndiaTourMap)
plugins.PolyLineOffset(coords, color="#00f", opacity=0.5, offset=5).add_to(IndiaTourMap)
#Let us show the map
IndiaTourMap.get_root().html.add_child(folium.Element(title_html))
IndiaTourMap

import numpy as np  # useful for many scientific computing in Python
import pandas as pd # primary data structure library
import folium
from folium import FeatureGroup, LayerControl, Map, Marker, features
import folium.plugins as plugins 
from folium.plugins import FloatImage, HeatMap, MarkerCluster, FastMarkerCluster, MeasureControl, MousePosition
from folium.features import DivIcon


loc = 'Continental USA Tour traversal in a Folium Map in a non-overlapping manner'
title_html = '''
             <h2 align="center" style="font-size:18px"><b>{}</b></h2>
             '''.format(loc)   
# Let us define a map with the US in the center and a reasonable Zool level with an Open StreetMap 
ContinentalUSTourMap = folium.Map(location=[40.0, -100], zoom_start=4, tiles="OpenStreetMap",scrollWheelZoom=False)

# Let us define Locations of the states to traverse in sequence. 
# These states are as per US Map. We can also use an algorithm on Latitude & Longitude for this as well
#

Locations = ['WA', 'OR', 'CA','NV','AZ','UT','ID','MT','WY','CO',
             'NM','TX','OK','KS','NE','SD','ND','MN','IA','MO',
             'AR','LA','MS','AL','TN','IL','WI','MI','IN','KY','OH',
             'WV','PA','NY','VT','ME','NH','MA','RI','CT','NJ','DE',
             'DC','MD','VA','NC','SC','GA','FL',
            ]

#Let us define the corresponding Latitudes and Longitudes for the capital cities of these states 
coords = [
    [47.042418,-122.893077],[44.931109,-123.029159],
    [38.555605,-121.468926],[39.160949,-119.753877],
    [33.448457,-112.073844],[40.7547,-111.892622],
    [43.613739,-116.237651],[46.595805,-112.027031],
    [41.145548,-104.802042],[39.7391667,-104.984167],

    [37.54,-77.46],[35.771,-78.638],
    [34.000,-81.035],[33.76,-84.39],
    [30.4518,-84.27277],
]

Capitals = ['Olympia','Salem','Sacramento','Carson City','Phoenix','Salt Lake City','Boise','Helena',
            'Cheyenne','Denver','Santa Fe','Austin','Oklahoma City','Topeka','Lincoln','Pierre',
            'Bismarck','Saint Paul','Des Moines','Jefferson City','Little Rock','Baton Rouge','Jackson','Montgomery',
            'Nashville','Springfield','Madison','Lansing','Indianapolis','Frankfort','Columbus','Charleston',
            'Harrisburg','Albany','Montpelier','Augusta','Concord','Boston','Providence','Hartford',
            'Trenton','Dover','Washington D.C','Annapolis','Richmond','Raleigh','Columbia','Atlanta','Tallahassee',
]
Population = [46478,174365,513624,55916,1680992,200567,228959,32315,64235,727211,
              84683,978908,655057,125310,289102,13646,73529,308096,214237,42838,
              197312,220236,160628,198525,670820,114230,259680,118210,876384,27679,
              898553,46536,49528,96460,7855,18681,43627,692600,179883,122105,83203,
              38079,39174,230436,474069,131674,506811,194500,32113,345064,
]
tiles = ['stamenwatercolor', 'cartodbpositron', 'openstreetmap', 'stamenterrain','stamentoner']
for tile in tiles:
    folium.TileLayer(tile).add_to(ContinentalUSTourMap)
#feature_group = FeatureGroup(name='Some icons')    
folium.LayerControl().add_to(ContinentalUSTourMap)
#Let us iterate and add the markers for the capital cities of each state we are traversing
iterlength = len(coords)
iteratorno = 0
iconc = folium.Icon(color="red",icon="fa-car", prefix='car',icon_size=(20, 20))
while iteratorno < iterlength:
    my_string = ' 2019 Population  : :<b> {} </b> <br>'.format(Population[iteratorno])
    my_string = my_string + ' State  : :<b> {} </b> <br>'.format(Locations[iteratorno])
    tootip_str = " Capital City <b>" + Capitals[iteratorno] + "</b><br>" + my_string
    ContinentalUSTourMap.add_child(
        folium.Marker(
            location=[coords[iteratorno][0], coords[iteratorno][1]],
            popup=my_string,
            icon=DivIcon(icon_size=(50,50),html='<div style="font-size: 6pt; color : blue">' + str(iteratorno+1) + '</div>',),
            tooltip = tootip_str,
            radius=10+Population[iteratorno]/100000, 
            color='black',
            fill=True,
            fill_color='yellow',
            fill_opacity=0.2,
        )
    )
    ContinentalUSTourMap.add_child(
           folium.CircleMarker(
            location=[coords[iteratorno][0], coords[iteratorno][1]],
            radius=10+Population[iteratorno]/100000, 
            color='black',
            fill=True,
            fill_color='yellow',
            fill_opacity=0.2,
        )
    )
    iteratorno = iteratorno + 1
 
#feature_group.add_to(ContinentalUSTourMap)
LayerControl().add_to(ContinentalUSTourMap)
plugins.PolyLineOffset(
    coords, weight=2, dash_array="5,10", color="red", opacity=1
).add_to(ContinentalUSTourMap)
plugins.PolyLineOffset(coords, color="#00f", opacity=1, offset=-3).add_to(ContinentalUSTourMap)
plugins.PolyLineOffset(coords, color="#080", opacity=1, offset=3).add_to(ContinentalUSTourMap)
ContinentalUSTourMap.get_root().html.add_child(folium.Element(title_html))
ContinentalUSTourMap.save("Continental_US_Tour_Map.html")

import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import folium
district_wise_census = pd.read_csv("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/kalilurrahman/datasets/main/district%20wise%20population%20and%20centroids.csv")
state_wise_centroid = pd.read_csv("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/kalilurrahman/datasets/main/state%20wise%20centroids_2011.csv")
state_wise_census = district_wise_census.groupby(by="State").sum()[["Population in 2001","Population in 2011"]].reset_index()
state_wise_census = state_wise_centroid.merge(state_wise_census, left_on="State", right_on="State")
#state_wise_census.head()
#district_wise_census.head()
tn_districts = district_wise_census[district_wise_census["State"]=="Tamil Nadu"]
center_lat = tn_districts.mean().Latitude
center_long = tn_districts.mean().Longitude
TNMap = folium.Map(location=[center_lat, center_long], zoom_start=6.5, tiles="stamenterrain",scrollWheelZoom=False)
tiles = ['stamenwatercolor', 'cartodbpositron', 'openstreetmap', 'stamenterrain','stamentoner']
for tile in tiles:
    folium.TileLayer(tile).add_to(TNMap)
folium.LayerControl().add_to(TNMap)
for district in tn_districts["District"].unique():
    district_census = tn_districts[tn_districts["District"]==district]
    str_2011_Pop = district_census["Population in 2011"].values[0]
    str_2001_Pop = district_census["Population in 2001"].values[0]     
    my_string = 'Population 2011 : :<b> {} </b>, <br> Population 2001 :<b> {} </b> <br>'.format(str_2011_Pop,str_2001_Pop)
    tootip_str = " District <b>" + district_census.District.values[0] + "</b><br>" + my_string
    folium.Marker(
        location=[district_census.Latitude.values[0], district_census.Longitude.values[0]],
        popup=my_string,
        tooltip = tootip_str,
        icon=folium.Icon(icon='info-sign', color="red"),
        draggable=False
    ).add_to(TNMap)
for district in tn_districts["District"].unique():
    district_census = tn_districts[tn_districts["District"]==district]
    str_2011_Pop = district_census["Population in 2011"].values[0]
    str_2001_Pop = district_census["Population in 2001"].values[0]     
    my_string = 'Population 2011 : :<b> {} </b>, <br> Population 2001 :<b> {} </b> <br>'.format(str_2011_Pop,str_2001_Pop)
    tootip_str = " District <b>" + district_census.District.values[0] + "</b><br>" + my_string
    folium.Marker(
        location=[district_census.Latitude.values[0], district_census.Longitude.values[0]],
        popup=my_string,
        tooltip = tootip_str,
        icon=folium.Icon(icon='cloud', color="blue")
    ).add_to(TNMap)
folium.Polygon(
    locations=list(zip(tn_districts.Latitude, tn_districts.Longitude))[1:22],
    popup="Path",
    tooltip = "Path",
    color="violet",
    fill_color="green"
).add_to(TNMap)
folium.Polygon(
    locations=list(zip(tn_districts.Latitude, tn_districts.Longitude))[1:12],
    popup="Path",
    tooltip = "Path",
    color="black",
    fill_color="yellow"
).add_to(TNMap)
TNMap

tn_districts = district_wise_census[district_wise_census["State"]=="Tamil Nadu"]
center_lat = tn_districts.mean().Latitude
center_long = tn_districts.mean().Longitude
TNPopMap = folium.Map(location=[center_lat, center_long], zoom_start=6.5,scrollWheelZoom=False)
tiles = ['stamenwatercolor', 'cartodbpositron', 'openstreetmap', 'stamenterrain']
for tile in tiles:
    folium.TileLayer(tile).add_to(TNPopMap)
for district in tn_districts["District"].unique():
    district_census = tn_districts[tn_districts["District"]==district]
    str_2011_Pop = district_census["Population in 2011"].values[0]
    str_2001_Pop = district_census["Population in 2001"].values[0]     
    my_string = 'Population 2011 : :<b> {} </b>, <br> Population 2001 :<b> {} </b> <br>'.format(str_2011_Pop,str_2001_Pop)
    tootip_str = " District <b>" + district_census.District.values[0] + "</b><br>" + my_string
    folium.RegularPolygonMarker(
        location=[district_census.Latitude.values[0], district_census.Longitude.values[0]],
        radius = float(district_census["Population in 2011"].values[0]/200000),
        rotation=0,
        color="green",
        popup=my_string,
        tooltip = tootip_str,
        fill_color="purple",
        fill_opacity=0.6,
        line_opacity=0.8,
    ).add_to(TNPopMap)
folium.LayerControl().add_to(TNPopMap)
TNPopMap

center_lat = state_wise_census.mean().Latitude-1.4
center_long = state_wise_census.mean().Longitude

m = folium.Map(location=[center_lat, center_long], zoom_start=5.3,scrollWheelZoom=False)

tiles = ['stamenwatercolor', 'cartodbpositron', 'openstreetmap', 'stamenterrain']
for tile in tiles:
    folium.TileLayer(tile).add_to(m)

for state in state_wise_census["State"].unique():
    state_census = state_wise_census[state_wise_census["State"]==state]
    lat, lon = state_census.Latitude.values[0], state_census.Longitude.values[0]
    population = state_census["Population in 2011"].values[0]
    str_2011_Pop = state_census["Population in 2011"].values[0]
    str_2001_Pop = state_census["Population in 2001"].values[0]     
    my_string = 'Population 2011 : :<b> {} </b>, <br> Population 2001 :<b> {} </b> <br>'.format(str_2011_Pop,str_2001_Pop)
    tootip_str = " State <b>" + state_census.State.values[0] + "</b><br>" + my_string
   
    folium.Rectangle(
        bounds=[(lat, lon), (lat+(population/7e7), lon+(population/7e7))],
        popup=my_string,
        tooltip = tootip_str,
        color="green",
        fill_color="blue"
    ).add_to(m)

folium.LayerControl().add_to(m)
m
